In addition to his playing ability, Lewandowski has also been praised for his outstanding work-ethic, fitness, mentality, and discipline, both on the pitch and in training, by pundits, players and managers.<sup id="cite_ref-Robert_Lewandowski:_how_he_became_the_most_prolific_striker_in_Europe_185-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Robert_Lewandowski:_how_he_became_the_most_prolific_striker_in_Europe-185">&#91;185&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-How_brilliant_is_Bayern&#39;s_Robert_Lewandowski_186-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-How_brilliant_is_Bayern&#39;s_Robert_Lewandowski-186">&#91;186&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Robert_Lewandowski_brings_goals_and_fortitude_to_Borussia_Dortmund_187-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Robert_Lewandowski_brings_goals_and_fortitude_to_Borussia_Dortmund-187">&#91;187&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Outside_football">Outside football</span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Personal_life">Personal life</span></h3>
<p>Lewandowski's father gave him the name Robert to make it easier for him when moving abroad as a professional footballer.<sup id="cite_ref-188" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-188">&#91;188&#93;</a></sup> Lewandowski's father, Krzysztof (died in 2005),<sup id="cite_ref-189" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-189">&#91;189&#93;</a></sup> was a Polish <a href="/wiki/Judo" title="Judo">judo</a> champion, and also played football for <a href="/wiki/Hutnik_Warsaw" title="Hutnik Warsaw">Hutnik Warsaw</a> in the second division.<sup id="cite_ref-background_190-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-background-190">&#91;190&#93;</a></sup> His mother, Iwona, is a former <a href="/wiki/Volleyball" title="Volleyball">volleyball</a> player for <a href="/wiki/AZS_Politechnika_Warszawa" title="AZS Politechnika Warszawa">AZS Warszawa</a> and later vice-president of Partyzant Leszno.<sup id="cite_ref-background_190-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-background-190">&#91;190&#93;</a></sup> His sister, Milena, also plays volleyball and has represented the U21 national team.<sup id="cite_ref-background_190-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-background-190">&#91;190&#93;</a></sup> He shares a surname with <a href="/wiki/Gina_Lewandowski" title="Gina Lewandowski">Gina Lewandowski</a>, an American defender for Bayern's women's team from 2012 to 2019, but is not known to be related to her.<sup id="cite_ref-191" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-191">&#91;191&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>His wife, <a href="/wiki/Anna_Lewandowska" title="Anna Lewandowska">Anna Lewandowska</a>, won the bronze medal at the 2009 <a href="/wiki/Karate" title="Karate">Karate</a> World Cup.<sup id="cite_ref-background_190-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-background-190">&#91;190&#93;</a></sup> They married on 22 June 2013 in the <a href="/wiki/Serock#Church_of_the_Annunciation_of_the_Blessed_Virgin_Mary" title="Serock">Church of the Annunciation of the Blessed Virgin Mary</a> in <a href="/wiki/Serock" title="Serock">Serock</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-wedding_192-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-wedding-192">&#91;192&#93;</a></sup> They have two daughters: Klara (born 4 May 2017)<sup id="cite_ref-193" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-193">&#91;193&#93;</a></sup> and Laura (born 6 May 2020).<sup id="cite_ref-194" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-194">&#91;194&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Lewandowski is a practising <a href="/wiki/Catholic_Church" title="Catholic Church">Catholic</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-195" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-195">&#91;195&#93;</a></sup> He met <a href="/wiki/Pope_Francis" title="Pope Francis">Pope Francis</a> in October 2014, when Bayern Munich visited <a href="/wiki/Vatican_City" title="Vatican City">Vatican City</a> following a 71 win over <a href="/wiki/A.S._Roma" title="A.S. Roma">A.S. Roma</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2014%E2%80%9315_UEFA_Champions_League_group_stage#Group_E" title="201415 UEFA Champions League group stage">UEFA Champions League</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-196" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-196">&#91;196&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In October 2017, the day after scoring to help Poland qualify for the 2018 World Cup, Lewandowski finished <a href="/wiki/Bachelor_of_Physical_Education" title="Bachelor of Physical Education">Bachelor of Physical Education</a> (BPhEd) with coaching and management at the Academy of Sport Education in Warsaw, concluding a decade of studies.<sup id="cite_ref-197" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-197">&#91;197&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-198" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-198">&#91;198&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-199" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-199">&#91;199&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In addition to his native <a href="/wiki/Polish_language" title="Polish language">Polish</a>, Lewandowski also speaks English and German.<sup id="cite_ref-200" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-200">&#91;200&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-201" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-201">&#91;201&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Philanthropy_and_business">Philanthropy and business</span></h3>
<p>Lewandowski and his wife, Anna, have supported, donated and raised money for various charitable organisations and for children throughout their career, including <a href="/wiki/Children%27s_Memorial_Health_Institute" title="Children&#39;s Memorial Health Institute">Children's Memorial Health Institute</a> in Warsaw, for which they've raised more than 150,000 <a href="/wiki/Polish_z%C5%82oty" title="Polish zoty">PLN</a> during Anna's birthday party on 25 August 2018.<sup id="cite_ref-202" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-202">&#91;202&#93;</a></sup> Lewandowski also donated 100,000 PLN for the treatment of Cyprian Gawe, a three-year-old boy from <a href="/wiki/Hel,_Poland" title="Hel, Poland">Hel</a>;<sup id="cite_ref-203" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-203">&#91;203&#93;</a></sup> and helps raising funds for the <a href="/wiki/Great_Orchestra_of_Christmas_Charity" title="Great Orchestra of Christmas Charity">Great Orchestra of Christmas Charity</a> each year, donating his personal items or private meetings that are sold at online auctions.<sup id="cite_ref-204" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-204">&#91;204&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-205" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-205">&#91;205&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-206" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-206">&#91;206&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In March 2014, he was named a <a href="/wiki/List_of_UNICEF_Goodwill_Ambassadors" title="List of UNICEF Goodwill Ambassadors">UNICEF Goodwill Ambassador</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-207" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-207">&#91;207&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In March 2020, Lewandowski and his wife, Anna, donated 1 million during the <a href="/wiki/2019%E2%80%9320_coronavirus_pandemic" class="mw-redirect" title="201920 coronavirus pandemic">201920 coronavirus pandemic</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-208" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-208">&#91;208&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Beside philanthropy, Lewandowski also invests primarily in <a href="/wiki/Startup_company" title="Startup company">startups</a>, <a href="/wiki/E-commerce" title="E-commerce">e-commerce</a> and websites, mainly through Protos Venture Capital, a company of which he is a shareholder.<sup id="cite_ref-209" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-209">&#91;209&#93;</a></sup> He also owns "Stor9_", an agency specialising in <a href="/wiki/Marketing_communications" title="Marketing communications">marketing communications</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-210" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-210">&#91;210&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Sponsorship_and_media_appearances">Sponsorship and media appearances</span></h3>
<p>In 2013, Lewandowski signed a sponsorship deal with <a href="/wiki/Nike,_Inc." title="Nike, Inc.">Nike</a>. Lewandowski plays in <a href="/wiki/Nike_Hypervenom" title="Nike Hypervenom">Nike Hypervenom</a> boots.<sup id="cite_ref-211" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-211">&#91;211&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Lewandowski featured on the cover of the Polish edition of EA Sports' <i><a href="/wiki/FIFA_15" title="FIFA 15">FIFA 15</a></i> video game, alongside <a href="/wiki/Lionel_Messi" title="Lionel Messi">Lionel Messi</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-212" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-212">&#91;212&#93;</a></sup> Lewandowski's "X" <a href="/wiki/Goal_celebration" title="Goal celebration">goal celebration</a>  arms crossed and index fingers pointing up  appears in <i><a href="/wiki/FIFA_18" title="FIFA 18">FIFA 18</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-213" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-213">&#91;213&#93;</a></sup>
</p>

<ul><li><span class="nowrap">1991: <a href="/wiki/Jean-Pierre_Papin" title="Jean-Pierre Papin">Papin</a> </span></li>
<li><span class="nowrap">1992: <a href="/wiki/Dennis_Bergkamp" title="Dennis Bergkamp">Bergkamp</a> </span></li>
